    (function() {
        'use strict';
        
        // List of tracking parameters that indicate user came from ads
        const TRACKING_PARAMS = ['fbclid', 'utm_source', 'utm_medium', 'utm_campaign', 'utm_content', 'utm_term', 'utm_id'];
        const STORAGE_KEY = 'has_tracking_params';
        const STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY = 'tracking_params_expiry';
        const EXPIRY_HOURS = 720; // 30 days expiration (30 * 24)
        
        /**
         * Check if URL has any tracking parameters
         */
        function hasTrackingParams() {
            try {
                const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
                for (let param of TRACKING_PARAMS) {
                    if (urlParams.has(param)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to parse URL parameters:', e);
            }
            return false;
        }
        
        /**
         * Check localStorage for tracking parameter history
         */
        function hasStoredTrackingParams() {
            try {
                const expiryTime = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY);
                if (expiryTime && Date.now() < parseInt(expiryTime)) {
                    const stored = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
                    return stored === 'true';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to read localStorage:', e);
            }
            return false;
        }
        
        /**
         * Save tracking parameter existence to localStorage
         */
        function saveTrackingParamStatus() {
            try {
                localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, 'true');
                const expiryTime = Date.now() + (EXPIRY_HOURS * 60 * 60 * 1000);
                localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY, expiryTime.toString());
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to save to localStorage:', e);
            }
        }
        
        /**
         * Redirect to clean version (without ads)
         */
        function redirectToCleanVersion() {
            // Get current path and construct clean version URL
            const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
            
            // Handle both cases: with and without .html extension
            let cleanPath;
            if (currentPath.endsWith('.html')) {
                // Replace .html with -clean.html
                cleanPath = currentPath.replace(/\.html$/, '-clean.html');
            } else {
                // Add -clean.html suffix
                cleanPath = currentPath + '-clean.html';
            }
            
            // Keep query string and hash if exists
            const search = window.location.search || '';
            const hash = window.location.hash || '';
            
            // Perform redirect
            window.location.replace(cleanPath + search + hash);
        }
        
        /**
         * Initialize version detection
         */
        function initVersionDetection() {
            // Check if current URL has tracking parameters
            const hasParams = hasTrackingParams();
            
            // If URL has tracking parameters, save to localStorage
            if (hasParams) {
                saveTrackingParamStatus();
                // User has tracking params, show ad version (no redirect needed)
                return;
            }
            
            // Check if localStorage has tracking parameter history
            const hasStored = hasStoredTrackingParams();
            
            // If both URL and localStorage don't have tracking params
            // Redirect to clean version
            if (!hasParams && !hasStored) {
                redirectToCleanVersion();
            }
            // Otherwise, user has stored tracking params, show ad version
        }
        
        // Execute detection immediately (before page loads)
        initVersionDetection();
    })();
    </script>

    })();

    <script>
    !function(f,b,e,v,n,t,s)
    {if(f.fbq)return;n=f.fbq=function(){n.callMethod?
    n.callMethod.apply(n,arguments):n.queue.push(arguments)};
    if(!f._fbq)f._fbq=n;n.push=n;n.loaded=!0;n.version='2.0';
    n.queue=[];t=b.createElement(e);t.async=!0;
    t.src=v;s=b.getElementsByTagName(e)[0];
    s.parentNode.insertBefore(t,s)}(window, document,'script',
    'https://connect.facebook.net/en_US/fbevents.js');

    fbq('init', '3902941096613787');
    
    // Natural 72-hour event tracking prevention (resets every 3 days)
    function shouldTrackEvent(eventName) {
        const now = new Date();
        const threeDaysAgo = new Date(now.getTime() - (3 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        const currentPeriod = Math.floor(now.getTime() / (3 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        const storageKey = `fb_event_${eventName}`;
        const lastTrackedPeriod = localStorage.getItem(storageKey);
        
        if (!lastTrackedPeriod || parseInt(lastTrackedPeriod) !== currentPeriod) {
            localStorage.setItem(storageKey, currentPeriod.toString());
            return true;
        }
        
        return false;
    }
    
    // Track PageView with 72-hour prevention
    if (shouldTrackEvent('PageView')) {
        fbq('track', 'PageView');
        console.log('Facebook event sent: PageView');
    } else {
        console.log('Facebook event skipped: PageView (already sent within 72 hours)');
    }
    
    // Reading time tracking for Facebook Pixel
    let readingStartTime = Date.now();
    let oneMinuteSent = false;
    let tenMinutesSent = false;
    
    function checkReadingTime() {
        const currentTime = Date.now();
        const readingTime = (currentTime - readingStartTime) / 1000 / 60; // in minutes
        
        if (!oneMinuteSent && readingTime >= 1) {
            if (shouldTrackEvent('1m_web')) {
                fbq('track', '1m_web');
                console.log('Facebook event sent: 1m_web (user read for 1 minute)');
            } else {
                console.log('Facebook event skipped: 1m_web (already sent within 72 hours)');
            }
            oneMinuteSent = true;
        }
        
        if (!tenMinutesSent && readingTime >= 10) {
            if (shouldTrackEvent('10m_web')) {
                fbq('track', '10m_web');
                console.log('Facebook event sent: 10m_web (user read for 10 minutes)');
            } else {
                console.log('Facebook event skipped: 10m_web (already sent within 72 hours)');
            }
            tenMinutesSent = true;
        }
    }
    
    // Check reading time every 30 seconds
    setInterval(checkReadingTime, 30000);
    
    // Also check when page becomes visible again (in case user switches tabs)
    document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', function() {
        if (!document.hidden) {
            checkReadingTime();
        }
    });
    </script>

    <!-- Tracking Parameter Persistence System -->
    <script>
    (function() {
        'use strict';
        
        // List of tracking parameters to persist
        const TRACKING_PARAMS = ['fbclid', 'utm_source', 'utm_medium', 'utm_campaign', 'utm_content', 'utm_term', 'utm_id'];
        const STORAGE_KEY = 'tracking_params';
        const STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY = 'tracking_params_expiry';
        const EXPIRY_HOURS = 24; // 24 hours expiration
        
        /**
         * Extract tracking parameters from URL
         */
        function extractTrackingParams(url) {
            const params = {};
            try {
                const urlObj = new URL(url);
                TRACKING_PARAMS.forEach(param => {
                    const value = urlObj.searchParams.get(param);
                    if (value) {
                        params[param] = value;
                    }
                });
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('URL parsing failed:', e);
            }
            return params;
        }
        
        /**
         * Save tracking parameters to localStorage
         */
        function saveTrackingParams(params) {
            if (Object.keys(params).length === 0) return;
            
            try {
                localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(params));
                const expiryTime = Date.now() + (EXPIRY_HOURS * 60 * 60 * 1000);
                localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY, expiryTime.toString());
                console.log('Tracking parameters saved:', params);
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to save tracking parameters:', e);
            }
        }
        
        /**
         * Read tracking parameters from localStorage
         */
        function loadTrackingParams() {
            try {
                const expiryTime = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY);
                if (expiryTime && Date.now() > parseInt(expiryTime)) {
                    // Expired, clearing
                    localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY);
                    localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_EXPIRY_KEY);
                    console.log('Tracking parameters expired and cleared');
                    return {};
                }
                
                const stored = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
                if (stored) {
                    const params = JSON.parse(stored);
                    console.log('Loaded tracking parameters from storage:', params);
                    return params;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to read tracking parameters:', e);
            }
            return {};
        }
        
        /**
         * Add tracking parameters to links
         */
        function addTrackingParamsToUrl(url, params) {
            if (Object.keys(params).length === 0) return url;
            
            try {
                const urlObj = new URL(url, window.location.origin);
                
                // Only process same-domain links
                if (urlObj.origin !== window.location.origin) {
                    return url;
                }
                
                // Add parameters
                Object.keys(params).forEach(key => {
                    if (!urlObj.searchParams.has(key)) {
                        urlObj.searchParams.set(key, params[key]);
                    }
                });
                
                return urlObj.toString();
            } catch (e) {
                console.error('Failed to add tracking parameters:', e);
                return url;
            }
        }
        
        /**
         * Process all links on the page
         */
        function processPageLinks(params) {
            if (Object.keys(params).length === 0) return;
            
            // Process all <a> tags
            const links = document.querySelectorAll('a[href]');
            links.forEach(link => {
                const href = link.getAttribute('href');
                if (href && !href.startsWith('#') && !href.startsWith('javascript:')) {
                    const newHref = addTrackingParamsToUrl(href, params);
                    if (newHref !== href) {
                        link.setAttribute('href', newHref);
                    }
                }
            });
            
            console.log(`Processed {0} links`);
        }
        
        /**
         * Initialize tracking parameter system
         */
        function initTrackingSystem() {
            // 1. Check if current URL has new tracking parameters
            const currentParams = extractTrackingParams(window.location.href);
            
            // 2. If new parameters exist, save them (new parameters take priority)
            if (Object.keys(currentParams).length > 0) {
                saveTrackingParams(currentParams);
                console.log('New tracking parameters detected and storage updated');
            }
            
            // 3. Load stored parameters (either newly saved or previously stored)
            const storedParams = loadTrackingParams();
            
            // 4. If parameters need to be persisted, process all page links
            if (Object.keys(storedParams).length > 0) {
                // Wait for DOM to fully load
                if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
                    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
                        processPageLinks(storedParams);
                    });
                } else {
                    processPageLinks(storedParams);
                }
                
                // Monitor dynamically added links
                const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
                    processPageLinks(storedParams);
                });
                
                observer.observe(document.body, {
                    childList: true,
                    subtree: true
                });
            }
        }
        
        // Execute initialization immediately
        initTrackingSystem();
    })();
    </script>
    
    <!-- Page Visit Statistics Code -->
    <script>
    // Page visit data collection
    function sendPageVisit() {
        // First get user IP address
        getUserIP().then(userIP => {
            const data = {
                page: window.location.href,
                userAgent: navigator.userAgent,
                userIP: userIP
            };
            
            // Send data to Google Apps Script (V7)
            fetch('https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycbzAUUO8RgiDJj3SYAt7Nd35ZzHw04VYGR88Nq4GFmAbl1xYmmkE9ArzD8x6mF_yYcf00A/exec', {
                method: 'POST',
                mode: 'no-cors',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(data)
            }).catch(error => {
                console.log('Analytics error:', error);
            });
        }).catch(error => {
            // If IP retrieval fails, still send other data
            const data = {
                page: window.location.href,
                userAgent: navigator.userAgent,
                userIP: 'Unknown'
            };
            
            fetch('https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycbzAUUO8RgiDJj3SYAt7Nd35ZzHw04VYGR88Nq4GFmAbl1xYmmkE9ArzD8x6mF_yYcf00A/exec', {
                method: 'POST',
                mode: 'no-cors',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(data)
            }).catch(error => {
                console.log('Analytics error:', error);
            });
        });
    }
    
    // Get user IP address
    async function getUserIP() {
        try {
            // Method 1: Use free IP API
            const response = await fetch('https://api.ipify.org?format=json');
            const ipData = await response.json();
            return ipData.ip;
        } catch (error1) {
            try {
                // Method 2: Backup IP API
                const response = await fetch('https://httpbin.org/ip');
                const ipData = await response.json();
                return ipData.origin.split(',')[0].trim();
            } catch (error2) {
                try {
                    // Method 3: Third backup API
                    const response = await fetch('https://jsonip.com');
                    const ipData = await response.json();
                    return ipData.ip;
                } catch (error3) {
                    console.log('IP retrieval failed, using Unknown');
                    return 'Unknown';
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Send visit data after page load
    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', sendPageVisit);
    } else {
        sendPageVisit();
    }
    </script>

            <h1 class="chapter-title">Chapter 338</h1>
            <div class="content font-medium">
                <p>Luis narrowed his long eyes, a trace of indulgence flickering before he swiftly veiled it. "Miss Brown,aren't you weary of playing the same card over and over?"</p>
                <!-- /22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_1 -->
                <div id="div-gpt-ad-1762511097410-0" style="min-width: 300px; min-height: 250px; text-align:center; margin: 20px 0;" data-guide-monitored="true" data-google-query-id="CL7VxNyp5JADFceL6QUdQa4kmw">
                  <script>
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1762511097410-0'); });
                  </script>
                <div id="google_ads_iframe_/22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_1_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none; width: 300px; height: 0px;"></div></div>
                <p>His tone carried the lilt of teasing, yet it bore no sting of sarcasm.</p>
                <p>Miranda caught the pretense of calm on his face,amusement bubbling quietly in her chest.</p>
                <p>Without hesitation, she reached for the wine glass in his hand, letting her fingertips brush deliberately across the back of his.</p>
                <p>Luis pressed his lips together, a tingling wave coursing through his chest.</p>
                <p>She raised the red wine to her lips, the liquid glossing them,lending her an air even more enchanting.</p>
                <p>Tilting her head, she blinked slowly and flashed a triumphant smile."The bait always works on the willing."</p>
                <p>Luis' gaze lingered on her, her cheeks prettily flushed from the alcohol. For an instant, his mind strayed back to the night they first crossed paths in that hotel corridor.</p>
                <p>He steadied himself, speaking again, his voice turning hoarse. "You're drunk, not thinking straight."</p>
                <p>Miranda chuckled, set the glass down,and without pause sank onto his lap.</p>
                <p>Luis stiffened instinctively, but her palm pressed lightly against his chest, halting him mid-motion-a gentle shove that sent him reclining back.</p>
                <p>She leaned closer,her hair brushing his cheek, a subtle spark crawling over his skin.</p>
                <p>"Luis, I'm perfectly clearheaded now, just as I was last time." Her whisper hovered at his ear, as though spilling secrets meant for no one else.</p>
                <!-- /22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_2 -->
                <div id="div-gpt-ad-1762511122729-0" style="min-width: 300px; min-height: 250px; text-align:center; margin: 20px 0;" data-guide-monitored="true" data-google-query-id="CL_VxNyp5JADFceL6QUdQa4kmw">
                  <script>
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1762511122729-0'); });
                  </script>
                <div id="google_ads_iframe_/22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_2_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none; width: 300px; height: 0px;"></div></div>
                <p>Her bewitching eyes held him fast, filled with a challenge veiled in seduction.</p>
                <p>Though the day still burned outside, the curtains were drawn, and only a lone floor lamp bathed the room in its amber glow, wrapping them in a cocoon of warmth and privacy.</p>
                <p>The air thickened, heavy with heat, as though the atmosphere itself caught fire. Luis locked eyes with her, his stare unreadable and deep as still water.</p>
                <p>He said nothing, simply watched her, jasmine lacing the air between them, his breath uneven, a surge of heat coursing through his body.</p>
                <p>Then,with undeniable force, he leaned forward and claimed her lips.</p>
                <p>...</p>
                <p>On the wide king-size bed, Miranda lay languid, her hair fanned across the pillow like seaweed drifting on a tide, her cheeks still faintly stained with blush.</p>
                <p>Her throat dry, she nudged the man beside her."I need some water."</p>
                <p>Her voice was husky, carrying the air of a spoiled princess issuing a command.</p>
                <p>Luis heard her, rose without a word, and walked away.</p>
                <p>Fresh from the bathroom, his upper body was bare,muscles taut, a towel slung around his waist, every movement betraying the sharp lines of his V-shaped abs.</p>
                <p>He returned with a glass of warm water and held it out to Miranda. Too lazy to move, she drank directly from the glass still in his hand.</p>
                <!-- /22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_3 -->
                <div id="div-gpt-ad-1762511150792-0" style="min-width: 300px; min-height: 250px; text-align:center; margin: 20px 0;" data-guide-monitored="true" data-google-query-id="CMDVxNyp5JADFceL6QUdQa4kmw">
                  <script>
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1762511150792-0'); });
                  </script>
                <div id="google_ads_iframe_/22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_3_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none; width: 300px; height: 0px;"></div></div>
                <p>"Want more?" Luis asked.</p>
                <p>Miranda shook her head, sinking back, her gaze wandering over him-broad shoulders, narrow waist,and eight-pack abs. Born to privilege, blessed with talent, and above all, dangerously handsome-he was the kind of man women called a prize.</p>
                <p>She tilted her head, a sly smile curving her lips, eyes sparkling like a fox with a secret. "Luis, I want to change the condition."</p>
                <p>Her tone was feather-light, teasing. "Instead of being my bed partner, why not be my boyfriend?"</p>
                <p>Luis was just about to set the glass down when her words halted him mid-motion.</p>
                <p>He paused,catching the playful lilt in her tone.</p>
                <p>Placing the glass aside, he leaned back against the headboard,reached for the pack of cigarettes on the bedside table, and pulled one free.</p>
                <p>With a click, the lighter flared blue.</p>
                <p>Narrowing his eyes, he lit the cigarette, drew deeply,and exhaled-white smoke drifting to shroud his face like a curtain.</p>
                <p>"You never say what you mean," he murmured, his voice low and rasped, thick with restraint. "Today, it was mutual consent."</p>
                <p>He hesitated, and then gave a wry chuckle. "If I ever let myself care, you'd strip me clean-down to the bone."</p>
                <p>Miranda's composure barely wavered, though her tone grew faintly rigid. "What do you mean? I'm a good person."</p>
                <!-- /22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_4 -->
                <div id="div-gpt-ad-1762511185949-0" style="min-width: 300px; min-height: 250px; text-align:center; margin: 20px 0;" data-guide-monitored="true" data-google-query-id="CMHVxNyp5JADFceL6QUdQa4kmw">
                  <script>
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1762511185949-0'); });
                  </script>
                <div id="google_ads_iframe_/22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_4_0__container__" style="border: 0pt none; width: 300px; height: 0px;"></div></div>
                <p>Luis neither agreed nor denied, his eyes steady on her,tinged with scrutiny.</p>
                <p>After a pause, he stubbed out the cigarette. "A bed partner works fine; I happen to need one. Will you take the role?"</p>
                <p>Miranda's brows shot up, eyes widening. What was this turn of events? The script had flipped entirely. She had planned to reel him in, yet here she was, the one caught in his net.</p>
                <p>"Me, a bed partner?" She bolted upright, voice rising,disbelief ringing in every word.</p>
                <p>Luis studied her startled face, a peculiar satisfaction settling over him. His lips curved, a mischievous smile surfacing, with a rogue's glint dancing in his eyes. He reached out,long fingers tipping up her chin.</p>
                <p>Leaning close, his breath mingled with hers, warm air pressing into the narrow space.</p>
                <p>"Not willing?" Luis asked softly, teasing in tone,echoing her earlier play. "You were more than eager in bed just now; I thought you'd jump at the offer."</p>
                <p>His gaze held hers captive, missing nothing in her shifting expression.</p>
                <p>Miranda felt her patience flare, heat rising from her ears down her neck. Not shyness, but a storm between reluctance and yearning.</p>
                <p>Inwardly, two tiny voices clashed. One cried it was absurd to accept; the other, bewitched, urged her to surrender.</p>
                <p>She bit her lip, caught in the tug-of-war.</p>
                <p>At last, she drew a long breath, as though sealing her choice.</p>
                <p>Her eyes lifted to his. "I can agree, but don't you dare regret it."</p>
                <!-- /22796784223/Netlink/myfreenovel.com/banner_5 -->
                <div id="div-gpt-ad-1762511205923-0" style="min-width: 300px; min-height: 250px; text-align:center; margin: 20px 0;" data-guide-monitored="true" data-google-query-id="CMLVxNyp5JADFceL6QUdQa4kmw">
                  <script>
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-1762511205923-0'); });
